<uploaded_files>
/testbed
</uploaded_files>
I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Simplify get-version string interface
Ever since PolarSSL in 3ac1b2d952ea200e66187c40e58729ebc84d8f11, the interface to get the PolarSSL then Mbed TLS version string has been:

```
/**
 * Get the version string ("x.y.z").
 *
 * \param string    The string that will receive the value.
 *                  (Should be at least 9 bytes in size)
 */
void mbedtls_version_get_string(char *string);

/**
 * Get the full version string ("Mbed TLS x.y.z").
 *
 * \param string    The string that will receive the value. The Mbed TLS version
 *                  string will use 18 bytes AT MOST including a terminating
 *                  null byte.
 *                  (So the buffer should be at least 18 bytes to receive this
 *                  version string).
 */
void mbedtls_version_get_string_full(char *string);
```

[As noted by Bence](https://github.com/Mbed-TLS/TF-PSA-Crypto/pull/367#discussion_r2214335274) this is fragile and overly complex. We could just return a global string instead.

(The macro isn't good enough because applications need the version of the library they're running on, not the version they were compiled against.)

We aren't going to change to constructing the version string dynamically from parts. That would take more code than the string. So we don't need the additional flexibility.

If we were doing this from scratch, I think we should make it
```
const char *mbedtls_version_get_string(void);
const char *mbedtls_version_get_string_full(void);
```
Both functions returning globals.

For the sake of applications that want to support both Mbed TLS 3.x and 4.x, we may want to maintain compatibility and introduce the new functions with the new name. On the other hand, application compatibility is already possible by calling `mbedtls_version_get_number()` first.


</pr_description>

    39	 */
    40	void mbedtls_version_get_string(char *string);
    41	
    42	/**
    43	 * Get the full version string ("Mbed TLS x.y.z").
    44	 *
    45	 * \param string    The string that will receive the value. The Mbed TLS version
    46	 *                  string will use 18 bytes AT MOST including a terminating
    47	 *                  null byte.
    48	 *                  (So the buffer should be at least 18 bytes to receive this
    49	 *                  version string).
    50	 */
    51	void mbedtls_version_get_string_full(char *string);

    54	 * \brief           Check if support for a feature was compiled into this
    55	 *                  Mbed TLS binary. This allows you to see at runtime if the
    56	 *                  library was for instance compiled with or without
    57	 *                  Multi-threading support.
    58	 *
    59	 * \note            only checks against defines in the sections "System
    60	 *                  support", "Mbed TLS modules" and "Mbed TLS feature
    61	 *                  support" in mbedtls_config.h
    62	 *
    63	 * \param feature   The string for the define to check (e.g. "MBEDTLS_SSL_SRV_C")
    64	 *
    65	 * \return          0 if the feature is present,
    66	 *                  -1 if the feature is not present and

    69	 */
    70	int mbedtls_version_check_feature(const char *feature);

   220	int mbedtls_version_check_feature(const char *feature)
   221	{
   222	    const char * const *idx = features;
   223	
   224	    if (*idx == NULL) {
   225	        return -2;
   226	    }
   227	
   228	    if (feature == NULL) {
   229	        return -1;
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    if (strncmp(feature, "MBEDTLS_", 8)) {
   233	        return -1;
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    feature += 8;
   237	
   238	    while (*idx != NULL) {
   239	        if (!strcmp(*idx, feature)) {
   240	            return 0;
   241	        }
   242	        idx++;
   243	    }
   244	    return -1;
   245	}

    97	static int redirect_output(FILE *out_stream, const char *path)
    98	{
    99	    int out_fd, dup_fd;
   100	    FILE *path_stream;
   101	
   102	    out_fd = fileno(out_stream);
   103	    dup_fd = dup(out_fd);
   104	
   105	    if (dup_fd == -1) {
   106	        return -1;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    path_stream = fopen(path, "w");
   110	    if (path_stream == NULL) {
   111	        close(dup_fd);
   112	        return -1;
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    fflush(out_stream);
   116	    if (dup2(fileno(path_stream), out_fd) == -1) {
   117	        close(dup_fd);
   118	        fclose(path_stream);
   119	        return -1;
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    fclose(path_stream);
   123	    return dup_fd;
   124	}
   125

   127	{
   128	    int out_fd = fileno(out_stream);

   444	/**
   445	 * \brief       Verifies that string is in string parameter format i.e. "<str>"
   446	 *              It also strips enclosing '"' from the input string.
   447	 *
   448	 * \param str   String parameter.
   449	 *
   450	 * \return      0 if success else 1
   451	 */
   452	static int verify_string(char **str)
   453	{
   454	    if ((*str)[0] != '"' ||
   455	        (*str)[strlen(*str) - 1] != '"') {
   456	        mbedtls_fprintf(stderr,
   457	                        "Expected string (with \"\") for parameter and got: %s\n", *str);
   458	        return -1;
   459	    }
   460	
   461	    (*str)++;
   462	    (*str)[strlen(*str) - 1] = '\0';
   463	
   464	    return 0;
   465	}
   466

   468	 * \brief       Verifies that string is an integer. Also gives the converted
   469	 *              integer value.
   470	 *
   471	 * \param str   Input string.
   472	 * \param p_value Pointer to output value.
   473	 *
   474	 * \return      0 if success else 1
   475	 */
   476	static int verify_int(char *str, intmax_t *p_value)
   477	{
   478	    char *end = NULL;
   479	    errno = 0;
   480	    /* Limit the range to long: for large integers, the test framework will
   481	     * use expressions anyway. */
   482	    long value = strtol(str, &end, 0);
   483	    if (errno == EINVAL || *end != '\0') {
   484	        mbedtls_fprintf(stderr,
   485	                        "Expected integer for parameter and got: %s\n", str);
   486	        return KEY_VALUE_MAPPING_NOT_FOUND;
   487	    }
   488	    if (errno == ERANGE) {
   489	        mbedtls_fprintf(stderr, "Integer out of range: %s\n", str);
   490	        return KEY_VALUE_MAPPING_NOT_FOUND;
   491	    }
   492	    *p_value = value;
   493	    return 0;
   494	}
   495	
   496	
   497	/**
   498	 * \brief       Usage string.
   499	 *
   500	 */
   501	#define USAGE \
   502	    "Usage: %s [OPTIONS] files...\n\n" \
   503	    "   Command line arguments:\n" \
   504	    "     files...          One or more test data files. If no file is\n" \
   505	    "                       specified the following default test case\n" \
   506	    "                       file is used:\n" \
   507	    "                           %s\n\n" \
   508	    "   Options:\n" \
   509	    "     -v | --verbose    Display full information about each test\n" \
   510	    "     -h | --help       Display this information\n\n", \
   511	    argv[0], \
   512	    "TESTCASE_FILENAME"
   513	
   514	
   515	/**
   516	 * \brief       Read a line from the passed file pointer.
   517	 *
   518	 * \param f     FILE pointer
   519	 * \param buf   Pointer to memory to hold read line.
   520	 * \param len   Length of the buf.
   521	 *
   522	 * \return      0 if success else -1
   523	 */
   524	static int get_line(FILE *f, char *buf, size_t len)
   525	{
   526	    char *ret;
   527	    int i = 0, str_len = 0, has_string = 0;
   528	
   529	    /* Read until we get a valid line */
   530	    do {
   531	        ret = fgets(buf, len, f);
   532	        if (ret == NULL) {
   533	            return -1;
   534	        }
   535	
   536	        str_len = strlen(buf);
   537	
   538	        /* Skip empty line and comment */
   539	        if (str_len == 0 || buf[0] == '#') {
   540	            continue;
   541	        }
   542	        has_string = 0;
   543	        for (i = 0; i < str_len; i++) {
   544	            char c = buf[i];
   545	            if (c != ' ' && c != '\t' && c != '\n' &&
   546	                c != '\v' && c != '\f' && c != '\r') {
   547	                has_string = 1;
   548	                break;
   549	            }
   550	        }
   551	    } while (!has_string);
   552	
   553	    /* Strip new line and carriage return */
   554	    ret = buf + strlen(buf);
   555	    if (ret-- > buf && *ret == '\n') {
   556	        *ret = '\0';
   557	    }
   558	    if (ret-- > buf && *ret == '\r') {
   559	        *ret = '\0';
   560	    }
   561	
   562	    return 0;
   563	}
   564	
   565	/**
   566	 * \brief       Splits string delimited by ':'. Ignores '\:'.
   567	 *
   568	 * \param buf           Input string
   569	 * \param len           Input string length
   570	 * \param params        Out params found
   571	 * \param params_len    Out params array len
   572	 *
   573	 * \return      Count of strings found.
   574	 */
   575	static int parse_arguments(char *buf, size_t len, char **params,
   576	                           size_t params_len)

    10	/* BEGIN_CASE */
    11	void check_compiletime_version(char *version_str)
    12	{
    13	    char build_str[100];
    14	    char build_str_full[100];
    15	    unsigned int build_int;
    16	
    17	    memset(build_str, 0, 100);
    18	    memset(build_str_full, 0, 100);
    19	
    20	    mbedtls_snprintf(build_str, 100, "%d.%d.%d", MBEDTLS_VERSION_MAJOR,
    21	                     MBEDTLS_VERSION_MINOR, MBEDTLS_VERSION_PATCH);
    22	
    23	    mbedtls_snprintf(build_str_full, 100, "Mbed TLS %d.%d.%d", MBEDTLS_VERSION_MAJOR,
    24	                     MBEDTLS_VERSION_MINOR, MBEDTLS_VERSION_PATCH);
    25	
    26	    build_int = MBEDTLS_VERSION_MAJOR << 24 |
    27	                MBEDTLS_VERSION_MINOR << 16 |
    28	                MBEDTLS_VERSION_PATCH << 8;
    29	
    30	    TEST_ASSERT(build_int == MBEDTLS_VERSION_NUMBER);
    31	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(build_str, MBEDTLS_VERSION_STRING) == 0);
    32	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(build_str_full, MBEDTLS_VERSION_STRING_FULL) == 0);
    33	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(version_str, MBEDTLS_VERSION_STRING) == 0);
    34	}
    35	/* END_CASE */
    36	
    37	/* BEGIN_CASE */
    38	void check_runtime_version(char *version_str)
    39	{
    40	    char build_str[100];
    41	    char get_str[100];
    42	    char build_str_full[100];
    43	    char get_str_full[100];
    44	    unsigned int get_int;
    45	
    46	    memset(build_str, 0, 100);
    47	    memset(get_str, 0, 100);
    48	    memset(build_str_full, 0, 100);
    49	    memset(get_str_full, 0, 100);
    50	
    51	    get_int = mbedtls_version_get_number();
    52	    mbedtls_version_get_string(get_str);
    53	    mbedtls_version_get_string_full(get_str_full);
    54	
    55	    mbedtls_snprintf(build_str, 100, "%u.%u.%u",
    56	                     (get_int >> 24) & 0xFF,
    57	                     (get_int >> 16) & 0xFF,
    58	                     (get_int >> 8) & 0xFF);
    59	    mbedtls_snprintf(build_str_full, 100, "Mbed TLS %s", version_str);
    60	
    61	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(build_str, version_str) == 0);
    62	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(build_str_full, get_str_full) == 0);
    63	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(version_str, get_str) == 0);

    34	                    uint8_t *in_params, size_t in_params_len,
    35	                    uint8_t **out_params, size_t *out_params_len)
    36	{
    37	    // psa_outvec outvecs[1];

    40	        exit(1);

    44	    invec.base = in_params;

    48	    uint8_t *receive = malloc(max_receive);
    49	    if (receive == NULL) {
    50	        fprintf(stderr, "FAILED to allocate %u bytes\n", (unsigned) max_receive);
    51	        exit(1);
    52	    }

    57	    outvecs[0].base = &actual_received;

    60	    outvecs[1].len = max_receive;
    61

    63	    if (status != PSA_SUCCESS) {
    64	        free(receive);
    65	        return 0;
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    *out_params = receive;
    69	    *out_params_len = actual_received;

    71	    return 1;   // success

    74	psa_status_t psa_crypto_init(void)
    75	{
    76	    char mbedtls_version[18];
    77	    uint8_t *result = NULL;
    78	    size_t result_length;
    79	    psa_status_t status = PSA_ERROR_CORRUPTION_DETECTED;
    80	
    81	    mbedtls_version_get_string_full(mbedtls_version);
    82	    CLIENT_PRINT("%s", mbedtls_version);
    83	
    84	    CLIENT_PRINT("My PID: %d", getpid());
    85	
    86	    CLIENT_PRINT("PSA version: %u", psa_version(PSA_SID_CRYPTO_SID));
    87	    handle = psa_connect(PSA_SID_CRYPTO_SID, 1);
    88	
    89	    if (handle < 0) {
    90	        CLIENT_PRINT("Couldn't connect %d", handle);
    91	        return PSA_ERROR_COMMUNICATION_FAILURE;
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    int ok = psa_crypto_call(PSA_CRYPTO_INIT, NULL, 0, &result, &result_length);
    95	    CLIENT_PRINT("PSA_CRYPTO_INIT returned: %d", ok);
    96	
    97	    if (!ok) {
    98	        goto fail;
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    uint8_t *rpos = result;
   102	    size_t rremain = result_length;
   103	
   104	    ok = psasim_deserialise_begin(&rpos, &rremain);
   105	    if (!ok) {
   106	        goto fail;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    ok = psasim_deserialise_psa_status_t(&rpos, &rremain, &status);
   110	    if (!ok) {
   111	        goto fail;
   112	    }
   113	
   114	fail:
   115	    free(result);
   116	
   117	    return status;
   118	}

   120	void mbedtls_psa_crypto_free(void)
   121	{
   122	    /* Do not try to close a connection that was never started.*/
   123	    if (handle == -1) {
   124	        return;
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    CLIENT_PRINT("Closing handle");
   128	    psa_close(handle);
   129	    handle = -1;
   130	}

   496	                         ser_params, (size_t) (pos - ser_params), &ser_result, &result_length);
   497	    if (!ok) {
   498	        printf("PSA_AEAD_ENCRYPT server call failed\n");
   499	        goto fail;
   500	    }
   501	
   502	    uint8_t *rpos = ser_result;
   503	    size_t rremain = result_length;
   504	
   505	    ok = psasim_deserialise_begin(&rpos, &rremain);
   506	    if (!ok) {
   507	        goto fail;
   508	    }
   509	
   510	    ok = psasim_deserialise_psa_status_t(
   511	        &rpos, &rremain,
   512	        &status);
   513	    if (!ok) {
   514	        goto fail;
   515	    }
   516	
   517	    ok = psasim_deserialise_return_buffer(
   518	        &rpos, &rremain,
   519	        ciphertext, ciphertext_size);
   520	    if (!ok) {
   521	        goto fail;
   522	    }

   524	    ok = psasim_deserialise_size_t(
   525	        &rpos, &rremain,
   526	        ciphertext_length);
   527	    if (!ok) {
   528	        goto fail;
   529	    }
   530	
   531	fail:
   532	    free(ser_params);
   533	    free(ser_result);
   534	
   535	    return status;
   536	}

    56	                     (get_int >> 8) & 0xFF);
    57	    mbedtls_snprintf(build_str_full, 100, "Mbed TLS %s", version_str);
    58	
    59	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(build_str, version_str) == 0);
    60	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(build_str_full, get_str_full) == 0);
    61	    TEST_ASSERT(strcmp(version_str, get_str) == 0);
    62	}
    63	/* END_CASE */
    64	
    65	/* BEGIN_CASE depends_on:MBEDTLS_VERSION_FEATURES */
    66	void check_feature(char *feature, int result)
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.

Let me also check if I need to copy the regenerated file to the source tree:

Actually, looking at the build output earlier, it said `Generating test_suite_version.c`. This means it's generating from the `.function` file to the build directory. The source tree file is just a pre-generated version. It's fine.

Now, let me think about edge cases:

1. **Backward compatibility**: The old functions took a `char *` and wrote to it. The new functions return a `const char *` pointing to a static string. This is a breaking change. But the PR description acknowledges this and says they want to make this change for Mbed TLS 4.x (the version in the test data is "4.0.0").

2. **Thread safety**: The old functions were thread-safe as long as different threads used different buffers. The new functions return a pointer to a global constant string, which is also thread-safe (it's read-only).

3. **Null pointer**: The old functions could crash if passed NULL. The new functions return a valid pointer always.

4. **The `string.h` include removal**: I removed it from version.c since `memcpy` was no longer needed. This is correct.

Everything looks good. Let me run the tests one final time:
